has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying
with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided
pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <span style="color: #000000"><ix:nonNumeric id="id3ff8b1e641224e0eb8255b6cd2a4f60b" contextRef="From-2020-11-09to2020-11-09" name="dei:EntityExTransitionPeriod" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#x2612;</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></div>
<div style="margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px;text-align: justify">

<div style="margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 6px; width: 100%; height: 8px; border-top: 1px solid #000000; border-bottom: 4px solid #000000;text-align: center">

2.02.&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;<br /><br /></span></div>

<div><span style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10">&#xA0;</span></div>

November 9, 2020, Celcuity Inc. (the &#x201C;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Company</span>&#x201D;) issued a press
release regarding the Company&#x2019;s financial results for the
third quarter ended September 30, 2020. A copy of the
Company&#x2019;s press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this
report and is incorporated herein by reference.</span></div>

pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange

<div id="pgbrk" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; text-indent: 0px; margin-right: 0px">
<div id="hdr">
<div style="text-align: right; width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
&#xA0; <font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="font-weight: bold">Exhibit 99.1</font><br></font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
&#xA0;Celcuity Reports Third Quarter 2020 Financial
Results</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
and Recent Business Highlights</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-style: italic; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
- New clinical trial collaborations with pharmaceutical companies
on track to close -</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-style: italic; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
- Cash burn rate steady -</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-style: italic; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
- Cash and cash equivalents of $13.7 million as of September 30,
2020, which is expected to support operations through 2021
-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-style: italic; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
&#xA0;- Conference Call on Monday, November 9th at 4:30pm (ET)
-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Minneapolis,
Minnesota&#x2014;November 9, 2020&#x2014;Celcuity Inc. (Nasdaq:
CELC), a clinical stage biotechnology company translating
discoveries of new cancer sub-types into 3<font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top">rd</font> generation
diagnostics and expanded therapeutic options for cancer patients,
announced financial results for the third quarter ended September
30, 2020 and summarized recent business progress.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x201C;During
the third quarter, we continued to advance our collaboration
discussions with pharmaceutical companies. We expect to close
several pharmaceutical company collaborations over the next few
months,&#x201D; said Brian Sullivan, Chairman and Chief Executive
Officer of Celcuity. &#x201C;Each collaboration will evaluate
different drug combinations in HER2-negative metastatic breast
cancer patients selected with our CELsignia Multipathway Activity
test. The collaborations we expect to close first will evaluate
patients with either hyperactive HER2 signaling tumors or those
with hyperactive c-Met and HER2 signaling tumors. Our discussions
with pharmaceutical companies to evaluate PI3K inhibitors in breast
or ovarian cancer patients with hyperactive PI3K signaling are also
progressing. These discussions are at an earlier stage than those
involving patients with hyperactive HER2 or c-Met signaling. We are
also very excited about the clinical investigators we expect to
partner with to field these trials. They are amongst the most
respected oncology researchers and thought leaders in the
country.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x201C;We
continued to make progress advancing additional new tests during
the quarter. Our goal is to develop new CELsignia tests that
identify RAS pathway driven cancers undetectable with molecular
tests in breast and ovarian cancer. Dysregulated signaling
involving RAS network nodes is responsible for a significant
percentage of all cancers, which has led many pharmaceutical
companies to sponsor research in this area.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x201C;Our
CELsignia platform also provides unique insights into the relative
potency and efficacy of the different therapies targeting RAS
nodes. This enables us to determine the relative superiority of the
different RAS-node approved and investigational targeted therapies,
which will help guide our collaboration activities.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#x201C;Finally,
we continue to expect interim results from our FACT-1 and FACT-2
trials in the second half of 2021. However, as you would expect, we
are monitoring the recent increase in COVD-19 related
hospitalizations for potential impact on enrollment activities for
these trials.&#x201D;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div id="pgbrk" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; text-indent: 0px; margin-right: 0px">
<div id="ftr">
<div style="text-align: left; width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
</div>
<div id="pb" style="text-align: center; page-break-after: always; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 6px; width: 100%; height: 1px; background-color: #000000">
<!--page break--></div>
<div id="hdr">
<div style="text-align: left; width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Recent Highlights and Upcoming Milestones</font></div>
<div><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Multiple clinical
trial collaborations amongst several major pharmaceutical companies
advancing towards close.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Data for two new
CELsignia tests in two different tumor types announced during past
nine months.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Expect to complete
development of a CELsignia RAS test for breast cancer patients by
next quarter.</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-left: 24px; display: table">
<div style="display: table-row">
<div style="text-align: left; display: table-cell; width: 24px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">-</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; display: table-cell"><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Interim results
from the FACT-1 and FACT-2 trials are expected in the second half
of 2021</font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Third Quarter 2020 Financials</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Total
operating expenses were $2.48 million for the third quarter of
2020, compared to $2.09 million for the third quarter of 2019.
Operating expenses for the first nine months of 2020 were $7.0
million, compared to $5.91 million for the first nine months of
2019.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Research
and development (R&amp;D) expenses were $1.96 million for the third
quarter of 2020, compared to $1.71 million for the third quarter of
2019. R&amp;D expenses for the first nine months of 2020 were $5.57
million, compared to $4.77 million for the first nine months of
2019. The approximately $0.80 million increase during the first
nine months of fiscal year 2020, compared to the first nine months
of fiscal year 2019, resulted primarily from a $0.71 million
increase in compensation related expenses, including approximately
$0.45 million of non-cash stock-based compensation expense. In
addition, other research and development expenses increased $0.09
million due to clinical validation and laboratory studies, and
operational and business development activities.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">General
and administrative (G&amp;A) expenses were $0.52 million for the
third quarter of 2020, compared to $0.38 million for the third
quarter of 2019. G&amp;A expenses for the first nine months of 2020
were $1.43 million, compared to $1.13 million for the first nine
months of 2019. The approximately $0.30 million increase during
fiscal year 2020, compared to fiscal year 2019, resulted primarily
from a $0.24 million increase in compensation related expenses,
including approximately $0.21 million of non-cash stock-based
compensation. In addition, other general and administrative
expenses increased $0.06 million primarily due to professional fees
associated with being a public company.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Net
loss for the third quarter of 2020 was $2.47 million, or $0.24 per
share, compared to a net loss of $1.98 million, or $0.19 per share,
for the third quarter of 2019. Net loss for the first nine months
of 2020 was $6.92 million, or $0.67 per share, compared to $5.55
million, or $0.54 per share, for the first nine months of 2019.
Non-GAAP adjusted net loss for the third quarter of 2020 was $2.03
million, or $0.20 per share, compared to non-GAAP adjusted net loss
of $1.68 million, or $0.16 per share, for the third quarter of
2019. Non-GAAP adjusted net loss for the first nine months of 2020
was $5.59 million, or $0.54 per share, compared to non-GAAP
adjusted net loss of $4.87 million, or $0.47 per share, for the
first nine months of 2019. Non-GAAP adjusted net loss excludes
stock-based compensation expense. Because this item has no impact
on Celcuity&#x2019;s cash position, <font style="color: #231F20">management believes non-GAAP adjusted net loss
better enables Celcuity to focus on cash used in operations.</font>
For a reconciliation of financial measures calculated in accordance
with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States
(GAAP) to non-GAAP financial measures, please see the financial
tables at the end of this press release.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">Net
cash used in operating activities for the third quarter of 2020 was
$1.65 million, compared to $1.48 million for the third quarter of
2019.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>

<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">At

<font style="color: #231F20; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
About Celcuity</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px"><font style="color: #231F20">
Celcuity is a clinical stage biotechnology company translating
discoveries of new cancer sub-types into pioneering companion
diagnostics and expanded therapeutic options for cancer patients.
Celcuity&#x2019;s 3</font><font style="font-size: 70%; vertical-align: top; color: #231F20">rd</font>
<font style="color: #231F20">generation diagnostic platform,
CELsignia, analyzes living tumor cells to untangle the complexity
of the cellular activity driving a patient&#x2019;s cancer. This
allows Celcuity to discover new cancer sub-types molecular
diagnostics cannot detect. Celcuity is driven to improve outcomes
for patients and to transform how pharmaceutical companies define
the patient populations for their targeted therapies. Celcuity is
headquartered in Minneapolis, MN. Further information about
Celcuity can be found at</font> <font style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0563C1">www.celcuity.com</font><font style="color: #231F20">.</font></font></div>
<div><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">

include, without limitation, expectations with respect to new

FACT 1 and FACT 2 clinical trials, clinical trial patient
enrollment and timing of results,</font> anticipated benefits that

<div style="text-align: left; width: 100%; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">

<div><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font>
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10"><br>
</font></div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #231F20; font-weight: bold; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
Cautionary Statement Regarding Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</font></div>
<div><font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10">&#xA0;</font></div>
<div style="text-align: left; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="color: #231F20; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">
This press release contains references to non-GAAP adjusted net
loss and non-GAAP adjusted net loss per share. Management believes
these non-GAAP financial measures are useful supplemental measures
for planning, monitoring, and evaluating operational performance as
they exclude stock-based compensation expense from net loss and net
loss per share. Management excludes this item because it does not
impact Celcuity&#x2019;s cash position, which management believes
better enables Celcuity to focus on cash used in operations.
However, non-GAAP adjusted net loss and non-GAAP adjusted net loss
per share are not recognized measures under GAAP and do not have a
standardized meaning prescribed by GAAP. As a result,
management&#x2019;s method of calculating non-GAAP adjusted net loss
and non-GAAP adjusted net loss per share may differ materially from
the method used by other companies. Therefore, non-GAAP adjusted
net loss and non-GAAP adjusted net loss per share may not be
comparable to similarly titled measures presented by other
companies. Investors are cautioned that non-GAAP adjusted net loss
and non-GAAP adjusted net loss per share should not be construed as
alternatives to net loss, net loss per share or other statements of
operations data (which are determined in accordance with GAAP) as
an indicator of Celcuity&#x2019;s performance or as a measure of
liquidity and cash flows.</font></div>
<div style="text-align: justify; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; text-indent: 0px">
<font style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 13px">&#xA0;</font></div>
